 The process of impeachment in the assembly against Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao of Karnataka has started so that the adamant Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao can be removed from his post if he does not resign
 wo desh ke pehle aise lokayukta honge, jinhen mahabhiyog ke jariye unke pad se hataaya jayega
 In fact, Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao has not been coming to office for the last three months, since his son Ashwin Rao has been accused of extorting about Rs 100 crore from government officials by showing fear of Lokayukta Red
 is maamle main hangaamaa uthne par sarkaar ne aiji level ke adhikari camel pant kii dekharekh main ek vishesh jaanch dal kaa gathan kiya tha, jisane asina raav ke saath-saath lokayukta daftar main tainaat sanyukt ayukta sayed riyaaz or unke ek mitra ko giraftaar kar jail bhej diya tha
 It is clear that Lokayukta Justice Bhaskar Rao was aware of this racket running from Lokayukta office and his official residence
 unase bhi esaiti ne is babat poochtacha kii he, lekin sanvaidhanik pad par asin hone kii vajah se unke khilaaf karrwai karne main kuch kanoonee pechidgiyaan aa rahi hai
 On the other hand, Bhaskar Rao has not resigned so far despite being so upset
 haalanki sarkaar kii taraf se unhen hataane kii har mumkin koshish kii gai

 Assuming an incident of misuse of biometrics data, the Unique Identification Authority of India (UIDAI) on Sunday said that all the information of the registered people is safe
 yuidiai kaa yah bayaan tab aayaa he jabaaadhara data main sendhamari kii khabarembar-baar aa rahi hai
 The Ministry of Electronics and IT said in a statement, "this is the first case of its kind that got caught in the internal security system of UIDAI and with that action has been started under the Aadhaar Act
 ‚Äômantralay ke anusaar, ‚Äôvibhinn print or soshal media main pichley kuch dinon main aa rahiaadhar data main send, biomitrix ke durupyog, niztaa main send or samanaantar data base ke srijan jaisi galat soochnaaon ke maddenjar yuidiai ne kaha he ki usne in reports ko dhyaan se dekha he or vah jor dekar kahana chaahati he ki aadhaar ke yuidiai databes main koi send nahin lagi he or yuidiai ke paas logon kaa vyaktigat data bilkul surakshit he
 According to the ministry, 'UIDAI is the most advanced encryption technology used for the transfer and hosting of data
 ' bayaan ke mutabik, 'iske parinamswaroop pichley saat saalon main yuidiai se kisi bhi naagarik ke data main send lagane kii koi khabar nahin ai he

 dekhe video Fraud in ATM or online transactions is increasing
 Most ATM fraud is being done through card cloning, this fraud can be avoided by taking some precaution
 Use of digital wallet requires careful use of ATM or online transactions
 
 noida main rahane vaale abhiranjan kumaar ravivaar ko apane ghar par aaraam kar rahe the, achaanak unke khate se 25 hajaar rupee cat jane kaa mobile par massej aayaa
 They were surprised
 unhen samaj main aa gaya ki unke saath thagi hui he
 Not only did he block his account, but also lodged a complaint with the cyber station, but the money has gone from the account, for which now he will have to fight with the bank
 aajkal kaaphi log cashles tranjaction kar rahe hai
 In such a situation, along with plastic cards, mobile and internet banking has also increased rapidly
 isi bich sibar krime kaa bhi khatra badha hua he
 If someone's hard-earned money flies in this way, then what can be passed on it can be understood
 isse bachane kaa kya he tarika or agar aisi thagi ho jaae to kya karnaa chahie, iske bare main aaie jaanate hai
 How do frauds are happening in many ways in this era of fraud from atms
 isamen pramukh he atm se hone vaala frod
 ATM fraudsters are so vicious that they withdraw money from people's atms while sitting far away
 peedit ko tab pataa chalata he, jab uske mobile par bank kii taraf se paise nikaale jane kaa massej aata he
 By the time the victim thinks something, their bank account is already empty
 aajkal sabase zyada atm frod, card chloning ke jariye kii ja rahi he
 To clone ATM cards, people go to the ATM machine and install a skimmer device
 ye skimar card swap karne vaali jagah ke upar lagata he
 It seems as if it is part of the ATM machine
 saath hi kii board ke upar ek bahut chota camera laga dete hai
 When the ATM card is installed in the machine, it clones it
 jab graahak apana code daal rahaa hota he to atm kaa password camere main darj ho jaataa he
 During this time there is no one other than the ATM card holder, but later the fraudsters clone the card through this and go away and withdraw money from the ATM anywhere
 isaki soochna asli atm card maalik ko tab pataa chalati he, jab uske mobile par tranjection massej aata he
 What should be the caution
 To avoid this type of fraud, you have to take some precaution
 jab bhi atm main jaaen, card swap karne vaali mashin ko hilaakar dekh le, agar wo hill rahi he to iskaa matlab kuch gadabad he
 Also, check the top side of the board properly whether there is any camera
 agar kuch gadabad najar aaye to fouran bank staff ko khabar karen
 What to do if your money is withdrawn from the ATM incorrectly After the new RBI rules, the responsibility of banks and customers in unauthorized transactions has been determined
 isamen digital madhyam se back khaaton kii sabhi lenden shaamil hai
 According to the new rule, the responsibility of a customer becomes zero if the unauthorized transaction is caused by the bank's mistake
 isamen sammilit frod, laaparvaahee, asweekruti jaisi tamaam chijen shaamil hai
 It is also not necessary to report to the bank for this
 yadi third party lenden ke dauraan bank yaa graahak donon kii hi galati na hokar, system main koi dosha ho or graahak is anaadhikrut lenden kii jaankaree bank ko teen kaamkaaji dinon ke bheetar de detaa he, to bhi uski deyta shunya maani jaati he yani bank ko puraa paisa waapas karnaa hoga
 The liability of a customer in unauthorized transactions varies from case to case
 yadi graahak dwaara laaparvaahee barti gai ho, masalan usne apane pement kii jaankaree kisi ke saath saajha kii ho or isaki jaankaree bank ko na di ho, to is sthiti main graahak ko hi puure nuksaan kaa sahanaa hoga
 In an unauthorized transaction, both the bank or the customer is not at fault, but even after the customer reports the system is delayed (four to seven business days), even in such a situation the liability of the customer is considered to be limited
 yadi report kii jaandaaree dene main saat kaamkaaji dinon se adhik kii deree ho, to graahak kii deyta bank ke board dwaara sweekrut policy ke aadhaar par hogi
 It is mandatory for banks to inform customers about this policy at the time of opening the account
 arabiai ke anusaar, bainkon ko is jaankaree ko saarvajanik karnaa bhi anivaary he
 Existing customers are also required to tell separately about this information or modifications in it
 is baar main adhik jaankaree ke liye aap arabiai kii website par bhi ja sakate hai
 Be careful in using mobile wallet, if you use digital wallet, then you have to take special care in it
 petm wolet kaa daawa he ki uske sabhi yugers ke wolet kaa insurance kiya jaataa he
 This will keep the money in the app secure and the company will compensate for the loss
 company ne logon ko bharosa dilaayaa he ki agar petm hack ho gaya, phone chori ho gaya yaa duusare frod se petm se paisa churaayaa gaya to waisi sthiti main company yugers paise waapas karegi
 First of all, you have to give information about money theft to Paytm, after this the company will investigate it in its own way and if the claim is true, it will return the money to the users
 haalanki iske time limit he yani paise udaae jane ke 12 ghante kii bheetar petm ko isaki jaankaree deni hogi
 Information about the theft of money can be given by calling the company's customer care number
 in sab ke alaava agar aapkaa phone yaa tablet chori hua he jisamen petm acount he to aisi sthiti main aapako thane main FIR karaani hogi
 After this, a copy of the FIR has to be shown as proof to Paytm
